Meridan rd. in between drove several roads in the immediate area.	This flock came out into a field--that we had learned earlier they had been recently feeding in--right      at sundown all together. All of these fields are private ground and it took a little work to get permission to go on them, however, most land owners were agreeable since we were not hunters. As we changed locations and approached the flock--got to within about 25 yards--it appeared that one or two males would move with several females. However these smaller groups did not get more than a few yards from the main flock. The males listed were all larger than the females and showed a red head. Four of the males showed obvious tufts of dark feathers protruding from their upper breasts. Two ranchers we talked to advised that this flock had been in the area for at least a couple of months and at one time had totaled around 60 birds but they had noticed a decline in the total number of birds recently. More photos are available by return e-mail.
